## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Grafana Dashboard JSON Model Version Migration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in grafana/grafana that implement dashboard JSON model versioning and migration: the dashboard version schema definitions, the DashboardMigrator, and the field-level migration functions that upgrade old dashboard JSON to the current schema version.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

- **`v2.go` through `v42.go`** — 41 individual schema version migration functions (V2–V42), each transforming the dashboard JSON map in-place

- **`errors.go`, `metrics.go`** — Error types and metrics middleware

//\\n15: // 1. DataQueryKind Structure Changes:\\n16: //    - v2alpha1: kind = datasource type (e.g., \\\"prometheus\\\", \\\"elasticsearch\\\")\\n17: //    - v2beta1: kind = \\\"DataQuery\\\" (hardcoded), group = datasource type, version = \\\"v0\\\"\\n18: //\\n19: // 2. \"The dashboard JSON model versioning and migration system in grafana/grafana (sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec) is implemented entirely under apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/.\\n\\n## Architecture Overview\\n\\nThe system has three layers:\\n\\n### 1. Core Migration Engine (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/)\\n\\n- **migrate.go**: The central orchestrator. Defines the `migrator` struct and the public `Migrate(ctx, dash, targetVersion)` function. The migration pipeline: (a) strips backend-only fields, (b) applies frontend defaults via `applyFrontendDefaults()`, (c) applies panel defaults, (d) ensures unique panel IDs, (e) runs the schema version migration chain (V2\u2192V42), (f) adds built-in annotation queries, (g) cleans up for save. Also exposes `Initialize(dsInfoProvider)` to wire in datasource info.\\n- **frontend_defaults.go**: Replicates the Grafana frontend's `DashboardModel` and `PanelModel` constructor defaults in Go, so backend migrations produce identical JSON to what the frontend would produce.\\n- **metrics.go**: Prometheus counters `MDashboardConversionSuccessTotal` and `MDashboardConversionFailureTotal` for tracking migration outcomes.\\n\\n### 2. Schema Version Package (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/)\\n\\n- **migrations.go**: Defines `SchemaVersionMigrationFunc` type, `MIN_VERSION=0`, `LATEST_VERSION=42` constants, `DataSourceInfo`/`DataSourceInfoProvider` interfaces, `GetMigrations()` (returns the map of version\u2192function for V2\u2013V42), and `GetSchemaVersion()` (extracts schemaVersion from dashboard JSON).\\n- **errors.go**: `MigrationError` and `MinimumVersionError` error types with constructors `NewMigrationError()` and `NewMinimumVersionError()`.\\n- **migration_utils.go**: Shared type-safe accessors: `GetStringValue`, `GetBoolValue`, `GetIntValue`, `GetFloatValue`, `ConvertToFloat`, `ConvertToInt`, `IsArray`.\\n- **datasource_utils.go**: `MigrateDatasourceNameToRef()` (mirrors frontend `migrateDatasourceNameToRef`), `GetDataSourceRef()`, `GetDefaultDSInstanceSettings()`, `isDataSourceRef()`.\\n- **v2.go through v42.go**: Individual schema version migration functions V2\u2013V42. Each file implements a `V{N}(ctx, dashboard)` function that transforms the dashboard JSON map in-place and sets `schemaVersion=N`. Notable migrations include: V2 (services.filter\u2192time/templating), V6 (pulldowns\u2192annotations), V7 (nav\u2192timepicker), V14 (sharedCrosshair\u2192graphTooltip), V16 (row-based\u2192grid layout), V28 (variable property cleanup), V33/V36 (datasource name\u2192ref migration using dsInfoProvider), V38 (table display mode cell options).\\n\\n### 3. API Version Conversion Package (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/conversion/)\\n\\nHandles conversion between Kubernetes API versions (v0alpha1, v1beta1, v2alpha1, v2beta1):\\n\\n- **conversion.go**: `RegisterConversions()` registers all bidirectional conversion functions with the k8s runtime scheme.\\n- **v0.go**: `Convert_V0_to_V1()` (calls `migration.Migrate()` to upgrade schema to LATEST_VERSION=42), `Convert_V0_to_V2alpha1()`, `Convert_V0_to_V2beta1()`.\\n- **v1.go**: `Convert_V1_to_V0()`, `Convert_V1_to_V2alpha1()`, `Convert_V1_to_V2beta1()`.\\n- **v2.go**: `Convert_V2alpha1_to_V0/V1/V2beta1()`, `Convert_V2beta1_to_V0/V1/V2alpha1()`.\\n- **v2alpha1_to_v2beta1.go**: `ConvertDashboard_V2alpha1_to_V2beta1()` and ~30 helper functions for converting the structured v2 schema (panels, queries, variables, layouts, annotations, field configs).\\n- **errors.go**: `ConversionError` type and `NewConversionError()` constructor.\\n- **metrics.go**: `withConversionMetrics()` middleware that wraps conversion functions with Prometheus metrics and structured logging.\\n\\n### 4.
